в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Technical Choice: Why HashiCorp Vault (not AWS Secrets Manager)?

Problem Solved:
1. Multi-Cloud: Vault works across AWS, GCP, Azure (not vendor-locked).
2. Dynamic Secrets: Database credentials rotated automatically.
3. Audit Logging: All secret access logged for compliance.

Use Cases Handled:
- Database credentials (PostgreSQL, Redis)
- API keys (Chainlink, Infura, Alchemy)
- PII encryption keys (per-investor)
- Smart contract deployer keys

Scaling Efficiency:
- Lease-Based Secrets: Short-lived credentials reduce exposure window
- Auto-Rotation: Credentials rotated automatically (no manual intervention)
- Access Control: Fine-grained policies (e.g., service can only read specific secrets)

Technical Choice: Why Safe (formerly Gnosis Safe)?

Problem Solved:
1. Treasury Security: Platform funds require multiple approvers for withdrawals.
2. Governance: Smart contract upgrades require multisig approval.
3. Audit Trail: All multisig transactions logged on-chain.

Use Cases Handled:
- Treasury withdrawals (3-of-5 for <$100K, 4-of-5 for $100KвҖ“$1M, 5-of-5 for >$1M)
- Smart contract upgrades (3-of-5 with 48-hour timelock)
- Emergency pause (2-of-3 security multisig)

Scaling Efficiency:
- Programmable: Safe SDK enables automated transaction building
- Integration: Integrates with existing DeFi protocols (Aave, Compound, Uniswap)
- Recovery: Social recovery options (guardians can recover lost keys)

Note: Gnosis Safe rebranded to "Safe" in 2025. Documentation may reference either name.

рҹ“„4.8 DevOps & Infrastructure Layer

4.8.1 DevOps Architecture

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ DEVOPS & INFRASTRUCTURE LAYER в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ CI/CD Pipeline в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (GitHub Actions) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Code Commit вҶ’ Lint вҶ’ Test вҶ’ Security Scan вҶ’ Build вҶ’ Deploy в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Lint: ruff, mypy (Python), eslint (TypeScript) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Test: pytest (90% coverage), jest (React) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Security: bandit, semgrep, Snyk в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Build: Docker images, Helm charts в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Deploy: ArgoCD (GitOps) to Kubernetes в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Kubernetes (EKS/GKE) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Horizontal Pod Autoscaler (HPA) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Cluster Autoscaler (add nodes when pods pending) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Pod DisruLPion Budgets (high availability) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Network Policies (micro-segmentation) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Infrastructure as Code в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (Terraform) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў VPC, Subnets, Security Groups в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў EKS Cluster, Node Groups в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў RDS PostgreSQL, ElastiCache Redis в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў S3 Buckets, CloudFront Distributions в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Monitoring & Alerting в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (Prometheus + Grafana) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Metrics: CPU, Memory, Disk, Network, Request Latency в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Logs: Loki (aggregated logging) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Tracing: Jaeger (distributed tracing) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Alerts: PagerDuty integration (critical alerts page on-call) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Technical Choice: Why Kubernetes (not ECS/Lambda)?

Problem Solved:
1. Portability: Kubernetes works across AWS, GCP, Azure, on-premise (not vendor-locked).
2. Scaling: Horizontal Pod Autoscaler scales based on CPU, memory, custom metrics.
3. Self-Healing: Failed pods automatically restarted; failed nodes replaced.

Use Cases Handled:
- Microservices deployment (FastAPI services)
- Batch processing (reporting, data aggregation)
- Stream processing (Kafka consumers, Flink jobs)

Scaling Efficiency:
- HPA: Scale pods based on CPU (>70%), memory (>80%), or custom metrics (requests/sec)
- Cluster Autoscaler: Add nodes when pods pending due to resource constraints
- Pod Anti-Affinity: Spread pods across nodes/availability zones for high availability

Technical Choice: Why Terraform (not CloudFormation/Pulumi)?

Problem Solved:
1. Multi-Cloud: Terraform supports AWS, GCP, Azure, Kubernetes (not vendor-locked).
2. State Management: Remote state (S3 + DynamoDB locking) enables team collaboration.
3. Module Ecosystem: Reusable modules for common patterns (EKS, RDS, VPC).

Use Cases Handled:
- VPC and networking (subnets, route tables, security groups)
- EKS cluster and node groups
- RDS PostgreSQL and ElastiCache Redis
- S3 buckets and CloudFront distributions

Scaling Efficiency:
- Workspaces: Separate environments (dev, staging, production) with same code
- Modules: Reusable infrastructure components (e.g., "eks-cluster" module)
- State Locking: Prevents concurrent modifications (DynamoDB locking)

Technical Choice: Why Prometheus + Grafana (not CloudWatch)?

Problem Solved:
1. Multi-Cloud: Prometheus works across AWS, GCP, Azure, on-premise.
2. Custom Metrics: Application-specific metrics (request latency, cache hit rate).
3. Alerting: Prometheus Alertmanager routes alerts to PagerDuty, Slack, email.

Use Cases Handled:
- Infrastructure metrics (CPU, memory, disk, network)
- Application metrics (request latency, error rate, throughput)
- Business metrics (transaction volume, active users, AUM)

Scaling Efficiency:
- Federation: Multiple Prometheus servers for large-scale deployments
- Recording Rules: Pre-computed aggregations reduce query load
- Alertmanager: Deduplication, grouping, silencing of alerts

5. Data Flow Walkthrough

рҹ“„5.1 User Onboarding Flow

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ USER ONBOARDING FLOW в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 1. User visits React marketplace в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 2. Connect wallet (MetaMask/WalletConnect) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 3. Complete KYC form (name, email, national ID, address) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 4. FastAPI Investors Service encrypts PII в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 5. PII stored in PostgreSQL (AES-256 encrypted) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 6. Encryption key stored in HashiCorp Vault в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 7. FastAPI Gateway Service submits KYC to Claim Issuer в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 8. Claim Issuer verifies identity (off-chain) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 9. Claim Issuer signs ONCHAINID claim в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 10. Claim hash stored on-chain (ONCHAINID contract) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 11. FastAPI updates investor.kyc_status = "verified" в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 12. User can now subscribe to tokenized assets в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Technical Choices:
- PII Encryption: AES-256-GCM with per-investor keys (Vault)
- ONCHAINID: Decentralized identity (claim hash on-chain, PII off-chain)
- Claim Issuer: Licensed KYC provider (Sumsub, Onfido, Jumio)

Scaling Considerations:
- Async Processing: KYC verification happens asynchronously (user notified when complete)
- Caching: KYC status cached in Redis (24-hour TTL)
- Rate Limiting: KYC submissions rate-limited (10 per minute per IP)

рҹ“„5.2 Token Subscription Flow

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ TOKEN SUBSCRIPTION FLOW в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 1. User selects asset in React marketplace в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 2. FastAPI Assets Service fetches asset metadata (cached in Redis) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 3. User enters subscription amount (in USDC) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 4. FastAPI Compliance Service checks: в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў User KYC status (verified?) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Jurisdiction whitelist (allowed?) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Investor cap (not exceeded?) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Minimum investment (met?) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 5. If compliant, React prompts wallet signature в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 6. User signs USDC transfer transaction в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 7. Smart contract receives USDC, mints ERC-3643 tokens в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 8. Transfer event emitted (captured by blockchain indexer) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 9. Indexer publishes event to Kafka (topic: transactions) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 10. FastAPI Trades Service consumes Kafka event в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 11. PostgreSQL updated (user token balance) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 12. Redis cache invalidated (user portfolio) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 13. WebSocket pushes update to React frontend в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 14. User sees updated portfolio balance в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Technical Choices:
- Compliance Check: FastAPI pre-validates before blockchain transaction (saves gas on failed transactions)
- Event Indexing: Blockchain indexer captures events (The Graph or custom indexer)
- WebSocket: Real-time portfolio updates (no page refresh required)

Scaling Considerations:
- Batch Processing: Multiple subscriptions batched in single blockchain transaction (gas efficiency)
- Kafka Buffering: Events buffered in Kafka if backend services fall behind
- Cache Invalidation: Selective cache invalidation (only affected user's portfolio)

рҹ“„5.3 Cross-Chain Bridge Flow

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ CROSS-CHAIN BRIDGE FLOW в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (Ethereum вҶ’ Polygon) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 1. User initiates bridge in React (select tokens to bridge) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 2. FastAPI Bridge Service checks compliance (KYC valid?) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 3. React prompts wallet signature (Ethereum) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 4. User approves ERC-3643 token transfer to bridge contract в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 5. Bridge contract locks tokens on Ethereum в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 6. Lock event emitted (captured by relayers) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 7. Relayers (5-of-9 multisig) observe event в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 8. Relayers sign attestation (Merkle proof of lock) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 9. Relayers submit attestation to Polygon bridge contract в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 10. Polygon bridge contract verifies signatures (5-of-9) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 11. Polygon bridge contract mints wrapped ERC-3643 tokens в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 12. Identity Registry state synced (Merkle proof of KYC claims) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 13. Compliance Module rules replicated on Polygon в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 14. User receives wrapped tokens on Polygon wallet в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ 15. User can now trade on Polygon (low gas costs) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Technical Choices:
- Lock-and-Mint: Tokens locked on source chain, wrapped tokens minted on destination
- Relayer Network: 5-of-9 multisig prevents single point of compromise
- Compliance Sync: Identity Registry state synced via Merkle proofs (O(log n) verification)

Scaling Considerations:
- Relayer Redundancy: 9 relayers in geographically distributed locations
- Rate Limiting: Bridge volume limited ($10M/day) to prevent exploit drain
- Emergency Brake: Compliance Officer can pause bridge if sync lag >4 hours

6. Scaling Strategy

рҹ“„6.1 Horizontal Scaling Per Layer

Frontend Scaling

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ FRONTEND SCALING в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ CloudFront CDN (50+ edge locations) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ React SPA (Static Assets) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Cached at edge for 1 year (versioned filenames) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў HTML cached for 5 minutes (stale-while-revalidate) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Gzip/Brotli compression в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Scaling Triggers: в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Traffic spike вҶ’ CloudFront auto-scales (no action needed) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Cache miss rate >20% вҶ’ Review caching strategy в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Scaling Limit: Unlimited (CDN scales automatically)

Backend Services Scaling

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ BACKEND SERVICES SCALING в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Kubernetes HPA (Horizontal Pod Autoscaler) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Pod 1 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Pod 2 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Pod N в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (FastAPI) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (FastAPI) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (FastAPI) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ CPU: 70% в”Ӯ в”Ӯ CPU: 75% в”Ӯ в”Ӯ CPU: 68% в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Mem: 80% в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Mem: 82% в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Mem: 79% в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–І в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ HPA Configuration: в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Min replicas: 3 (high availability) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Max replicas: 50 (cost control) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Target CPU: 70% в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Target Memory: 80% в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Scale-up cooldown: 3 minutes в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Scale-down cooldown: 10 minutes в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Scaling Triggers: в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў CPU >70% for 3 minutes вҶ’ Add pods (up to 50) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Memory >80% for 3 minutes вҶ’ Add pods (up to 50) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Requests/sec >1000 per pod вҶ’ Add pods (up to 50) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Scaling Limit: 50 pods Г— 10,000 req/sec = 500,000 req/sec

Database Scaling

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ DATABASE SCALING в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ PostgreSQL Primary (Read-Write) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў 8 vCPU, 64GB RAM, 1TB NVMe в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Multi-AZ deployment (synchronous replication) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј (Async Replication) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ PostgreSQL Read Replica 1 (Read-Only) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў 4 vCPU, 32GB RAM, 1TB NVMe в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в–ј (Async Replication) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ PostgreSQL Read Replica 2 (Read-Only) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў 4 vCPU, 32GB RAM, 1TB NVMe в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Scaling Triggers: в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Primary CPU >80% вҶ’ Add read replica в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Storage >80% вҶ’ Add Citus worker node (sharding) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Write throughput >10,000/sec вҶ’ Consider sharding в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Partitioning Strategy: в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў transactions: partitioned by month (100M+ rows) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў audit_logs: partitioned by month в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў assets: partitioned by asset_type в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Scaling Limit:
- Read scaling: Unlimited (add read replicas)
- Write scaling: ~10,000 writes/sec (single primary); shard with Citus for more

Cache Scaling

в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ CACHE SCALING в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Redis Cluster (6 nodes: 3 masters, 3 replicas) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Master 1 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Master 2 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Master 3 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (5,461 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (5,461 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ (5,461 в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ slots) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ slots) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ slots) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”ӮReplicaв”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”ӮReplicaв”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”ӮReplicaв”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Scaling Triggers: в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Memory >80% вҶ’ Add new master node (rebalance slots) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў CPU >80% вҶ’ Add replica for read scaling в”Ӯ в”Ӯ вҖў Connections >10,000 вҶ’ Add proxy (Twemproxy/Codis) в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Hit Rate Target: >85% в”Ӯ в”Ӯ Alert: Hit rate <80% for 10 minutes в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

Scaling Limit: 16,384 hash slots Г— 3 masters = ~50GB data, 100,000+ ops/sec

рҹ“„6.2 Scaling Bottlenecks & Mitigation

Bottleneck Symptom Mitigation
Database Write Throughput Write latency >100ms, connection queue Add read replicas, partition tables, shard with Citus
Kafka Consumer Lag Consumer lag >10,000 messages Add consumer instances, increase partitions
Blockchain Gas Spikes Transaction failures, high gas costs Shift load to Polygon, batch transactions
Cache Miss Rate Cache hit rate <80%, database load spikes Review TTLs, warm cache on deployment
API Rate Limiting 429 Too Many Requests errors Increase rate limits, add caching
WebSocket Connections Connection drops, high memory usage Add WebSocket proxy (Socket.IO with Redis adapter)

7. Failure Modes & Recovery

рҹ“„7.1 Failure Mode Analysis

Failure Mode 1: PostgreSQL Primary Failure

Detection:
- Prometheus alert: postgres_primary_unreachable
- Application logs: Database connection errors

Automatic Recovery:
1. Kubernetes detects pod failure, restarts pod
2. If node failure, Kubernetes schedules pod on healthy node
3. RDS Multi-AZ fails over to standby (60вҖ“120 seconds)

Manual Recovery:
1. Promote read replica to primary (ALTER SYSTEM SET primary_standby_mode = off)
2. Update application connection string
3. Investigate root cause

Data Loss Risk: Minimal (synchronous replication to standby)

Failure Mode 2: Kafka Broker Failure

Detection:
- Prometheus alert: kafka_broker_down
- Consumer lag increasing

Automatic Recovery:
1. Kafka replicates partitions across 3 brokers (replication factor = 3)
2. If broker fails, partitions fail over to replicas
3. Kubernetes restarts failed broker pod

Manual Recovery:
1. Add new broker if cluster under-replicated
2. Rebalance partitions if needed

Data Loss Risk: None (replication factor = 3, min.insync.replicas = 2)

Failure Mode 3: Blockchain Gateway Failure

Detection:
- Prometheus alert: gateway_price_stale (no update >1 hour)
- Circuit breaker triggered (price deviation >5%)

Automatic Recovery:
1. Fallback to secondary Gateway (Pyth Network)
2. If secondary fails, use custom FastAPI Gateway
3. If all fail, pause trading (circuit breaker)

Manual Recovery:
1. Investigate Gateway provider status
2. Switch to backup Gateway provider
3. Resume trading when Gateway healthy

Data Loss Risk: None (Gateway data is ephemeral, can be re-fetched)

Failure Mode 4: Smart Contract Vulnerability

Detection:
- Bug bounty report (Immunefi)
- Unusual transaction patterns (fraud detection)
- Third-party audit finding

Automatic Recovery:
1. Emergency pause function (2-of-3 security multisig)
2. Trading halted, withdrawals paused

Manual Recovery:
1. Deploy patched smart contract (via upgradeable proxy)
2. Migrate state to new implementation
3. Resume trading after verification

Data Loss Risk: Depends on vulnerability severity (pause prevents further loss)

8. Technology Decision Matrix

рҹ“„8.1 Technology Selection Criteria

Technology Alternatives Considered Selection Rationale
Blockchain Ethereum, Solana, Avalanche, Polygon Ethereum (security) + Polygon (cost) dual-chain optimal for compliance + retail
Token Standard ERC-20, ERC-721, ERC-1155, ERC-3643 ERC-3643 only standard with built-in compliance (KYC, transfer restrictions)
Smart Contract Framework Hardhat, Truffle, Foundry, ApeWorX ApeWorX (Python integration, pytest, unified stack with backend)
Backend Framework Django, Flask, FastAPI, Node.js FastAPI (async, type safety, performance, Python ecosystem)
Database MySQL, PostgreSQL, MongoDB, CockroachDB PostgreSQL (ACID, JSONB, partitioning, mature ecosystem)
Cache Memcached, Redis, Hazelcast Redis (data structures, pub/sub, persistence, cluster mode)
Event Streaming RabbitMQ, Apache Kafka, AWS Kinesis Kafka (throughput, partitioning, replayability, ecosystem)
Frontend Vue, Angular, React, Svelte React (ecosystem, developer availability, component model)
Container Orchestration Docker Swarm, Kubernetes, ECS Kubernetes (portability, ecosystem, auto-scaling)
Infrastructure as Code CloudFormation, Pulumi, Terraform Terraform (multi-cloud, modules, state management)
Monitoring CloudWatch, Datadog, Prometheus Prometheus (open-source, multi-cloud, custom metrics)
Secrets Management AWS Secrets Manager, Azure Key Vault, HashiCorp Vault Vault (multi-cloud, dynamic secrets, audit logging)
